"Good morning."

A voice from beside me made my heart nearly stop.

I tried to turn my head toward her, but it felt like it would creak like a rusty machine.

[ILLUSTRATION: illust-001.jpg]

The first thing I saw were her blue eyes. As blue as the ocean, so deep you felt like you could be drawn into them forever.

Next came her snow-white hair and skin. Her hair was whiter, of course, but her skin was as pale as milk, reminding me of an innocent child. The whiteness wasn't sickly at all; if anything, it had the delicate, transparent quality of spun sugar.

And her sharp, chiseled features gave her a dignified air. Her expression was, as usual, almost unchanging. She could be seen as beautiful, or as cute.

"â€¦Excuse me."

Her soft, bell-like voice brought me back to my senses.

Damn, I'd been staring.

Left with no other choice, I began to walk.
I had never been to this area before. The scenery was new to me, a rarity that had me gazing curiously at my surroundings.
*I wonder if this would be more fun if Souta-kun were with me?*
The thought crossed my mind before I could stop it. I wondered if he might have shown me around if he were here. No... I was certain that simply having him by my side would be enough to put me at ease and bring me joy.
But he wasn't by my side. The mere realization sent a sharp pang through my chest, as if I had been pricked by a needle.
I pursed my lips tightly for a moment, then resumed walking.
That was when a particular shop caught my eye. At first glance, it looked like a cafÃ©, but something was slightly different. Upon closer inspection, it appeared to be a specialty sweets shop.
According to the banners displayed outside, a Mont Blanc fair was running until today. Once again, I couldn't help but think:
*...I wish I could have gone with Souta-kun.*
I murmured the words aloud, then immediately shook my head to dismiss them. His high school was nearby. If we were seen eating together, people might get the wrong idea. Rumors about Souta-kun and me were already on the verge of surfacing as it was. I didn't want to cause him any trouble.
Just as I was thinking it was time to head back...

I had never been to this area before. The scenery was new to me, a rarity that had me gazing curiously at my surroundings.

Left with no other choice, I began to walk.
I had never been to this area before. The scenery was new to me, a rarity that had me gazing curiously at my surroundings.
*I wonder if this would be more fun if Souta-kun were with me?*
The thought crossed my mind before I could stop it. I wondered if he might have shown me around if he were here. No... I was certain that simply having him by my side would be enough to put me at ease and bring me joy.
But he wasn't by my side. The mere realization sent a sharp pang through my chest, as if I had been pricked by a needle.
I pursed my lips tightly for a moment, then resumed walking.
That was when a particular shop caught my eye. At first glance, it looked like a cafÃ©, but something was slightly different. Upon closer inspection, it appeared to be a specialty sweets shop.
According to the banners displayed outside, a Mont Blanc fair was running until today. Once again, I couldn't help but think:
*...I wish I could have gone with Souta-kun.*
I murmured the words aloud, then immediately shook my head to dismiss them. His high school was nearby. If we were seen eating together, people might get the wrong idea. Rumors about Souta-kun and me were already on the verge of surfacing as it was. I didn't want to cause him any trouble.
Just as I was thinking it was time to head back...

Ah. So this was the place. The place he had mentioned.
*Tight.* A sudden constriction gripped me. My chest hurt, as if my heart were being wrung dry.

Left with no other choice, I began to walk.
I had never been to this area before. The scenery was new to me, a rarity that had me gazing curiously at my surroundings.
*I wonder if this would be more fun if Souta-kun were with me?*
The thought crossed my mind before I could stop it. I wondered if he might have shown me around if he were here. No... I was certain that simply having him by my side would be enough to put me at ease and bring me joy.
But he wasn't by my side. The mere realization sent a sharp pang through my chest, as if I had been pricked by a needle.
I pursed my lips tightly for a moment, then resumed walking.
That was when a particular shop caught my eye. At first glance, it looked like a cafÃ©, but something was slightly different. Upon closer inspection, it appeared to be a specialty sweets shop.
According to the banners displayed outside, a Mont Blanc fair was running until today. Once again, I couldn't help but think:
*...I wish I could have gone with Souta-kun.*
I murmured the words aloud, then immediately shook my head to dismiss them. His high school was nearby. If we were seen eating together, people might get the wrong idea. Rumors about Souta-kun and me were already on the verge of surfacing as it was. I didn't want to cause him any trouble.
Just as I was thinking it was time to head back...

Left with no other choice, I began to walk.
I had never been to this area before. The scenery was new to me, a rarity that had me gazing curiously at my surroundings.
*I wonder if this would be more fun if Souta-kun were with me?*
The thought crossed my mind before I could stop it. I wondered if he might have shown me around if he were here. No... I was certain that simply having him by my side would be enough to put me at ease and bring me joy.
But he wasn't by my side. The mere realization sent a sharp pang through my chest, as if I had been pricked by a needle.
I pursed my lips tightly for a moment, then resumed walking.
That was when a particular shop caught my eye. At first glance, it looked like a cafÃ©, but something was slightly different. Upon closer inspection, it appeared to be a specialty sweets shop.
According to the banners displayed outside, a Mont Blanc fair was running until today. Once again, I couldn't help but think:
*...I wish I could have gone with Souta-kun.*
I murmured the words aloud, then immediately shook my head to dismiss them. His high school was nearby. If we were seen eating together, people might get the wrong idea. Rumors about Souta-kun and me were already on the verge of surfacing as it was. I didn't want to cause him any trouble.
Just as I was thinking it was time to head back...

I murmured the words aloud, then immediately shook my head to dismiss them. His high school was nearby. If we were seen eating together, people might get the wrong idea. Rumors about Souta-kun and me were already on the verge of surfacing as it was. I didn't want to cause him any trouble.
Just as I was thinking it was time to head back...

Ah. So this was the place. The place he had mentioned.
*Tight.* A sudden constriction gripped me. My chest hurt, as if my heart were being wrung dry.

Her voice carried a slight bounce, brushing against my eardrums with a shivering, tactile caress. My heart began to pound alarmingly loud, and impossible options floated through my mind.

"...I... don't know."

"Is that so? That is a shame."

She said it was a shame, yet I couldn't sense any disappointment in her voice. Far from itâ€”she actually looked like she was having a little fun.

"Well then, please do let me know when you figure it out."

The answer I'd imagined didn't come, and a small sigh escaped me.

"So you aren't going to tell me."

"Fufu. For now, it is a secret."

Shinonome smiled slightly. Ever so slightly. Her peach-colored lips, vivid against her porcelain skin, parted to reveal a glimpse of her small, red tongue.

"Why do you think that is?"

Her voice carried a slight bounce, brushing against my eardrums with a spine-tingling rasp. My heart began to pound alarmingly loud, and impossible options floated through my mind.

"...I... don't know."

"Is that so? That is a shame."

She said it was a shame, yet I couldn't sense any disappointment in her voice. Far from itâ€”she actually looked like she was having a little fun.

"Well then, please do let me know when you figure it out."

The answer I'd imagined didn't come, and a small sigh escaped me.

"So you aren't going to tell me."

"Fufu. For now, it is a secret."

I'll stick to "Pressing a single finger against her lips".

Shinonome smiled slightly. Ever so slightly. Her peach-colored lips, vivid against her porcelain skin, parted to reveal a glimpse of her small, red tongue.

"Why do you think that is?"

Her voice carried a slight bounce, brushing against my eardrums with a spine-tingling rasp. My heart began to pound alarmingly loud, and impossible options floated through my mind.

"...I... don't know."

"Is that so? That is a shame."

She said it was a shame, yet I couldn't sense any disappointment in her voice. Far from itâ€”she actually looked like she was having a little fun.

"Well then, please do let me know when you figure it out."

The answer I'd imagined didn't come, and a small sigh escaped me.

"So you aren't going to tell me."

"Fufu. For now, it is a secret."

Her voice carried a slight bounce, brushing against my eardrums with a spine-tingling rasp. My heart began to pound alarmingly loud, and impossible options floated through my mind.

"...I... don't know."

"Is that so? That is a shame."

She said it was a shame, yet I couldn't sense any disappointment in her voice. Far from itâ€”she actually looked like she was having a little fun.

"Well then, please do let me know when you figure it out."

The answer I'd imagined didn't come, and a small sigh escaped me.

"So you aren't going to tell me."

"Fufu. For now, it is a secret."

Shinonome smiled, pressing a single finger against her lips.
My heart slammed violently against my chest.

"Stroking my eardrums".
"Brushing against" is more idiomatic for sound/voice.
I'll stick to "Brushing against".

Done.

"...I... don't know."

"Is that so? That is a shame."

She said it was a shame, yet I couldn't sense any disappointment in her voice. Far from itâ€”she actually looked like she was having a little fun.

"Well then, please do let me know when you figure it out."

The answer I'd imagined didn't come, and a small sigh escaped me.

"So you aren't going to tell me."

"Fufu. For now, it is a secret."

Her voice carried a slight bounce, brushing against my eardrums with a spine-tingling rasp. My heart began to pound alarmingly loud, and impossible options floated through my mind.

"...I... don't know."

"Is that so? That is a shame."

She said it was a shame, yet I couldn't sense any disappointment in her voice. Far from itâ€”she actually looked like she was having a little fun.

"Well then, please do let me know when you figure it out."

The answer I'd imagined didn't come, and a small sigh escaped me.

"So you aren't going to tell me."

"Fufu. For now, it is a secret."

[ILLUSTRATION: illust-004.jpg]

Shinonome smiled, pressing a single finger against her lips.
My heart slammed violently against my chest.

(Done.)

One note: "Lips front finger one stand-te" -> "Pressing a single finger against her lips".
"Against her lips" matches the illustration.
"Before her lips" matches the text.
But "Pressing against" is better English.
I'll stick to "Pressing a single finger against her lips".

Okay.

Final.

Shinonome smiled slightly. Ever so slightly. Her peach-colored lips, vivid against her porcelain skin, parted to reveal a glimpse of her small, red tongue.

"Why do you think that is?"

Her voice carried a slight bounce, brushing against my eardrums with a spine-tingling rasp. My heart began to pound alarmingly loud, and impossible options floated through my mind.

"...I... don't know."

"Is that so? That is a shame."

She said it was a shame, yet I couldn't sense any disappointment in her voice. Far from itâ€”she actually looked like she was having a little fun.

"Well then, please do let me know when you figure it out."

The answer I'd imagined didn't come, and a small sigh escaped me.

"So you aren't going to tell me."

"Fufu. For now, it is a secret."
